          13
          
                arel.group(*@group_values.uniq.reject{|g| g.blank?}) unless @group_values.empty?
        
      276. 
      
        
    276. 
          
          
          
        
      277. 
      
        
    277. 
          13
          
                order = @order_values
        
      278. 
      
        
    278. 
          13
          
                order = reverse_sql_order(order) if @reverse_order_value
        
      279. 
      
        
    279. 
          13
          
                arel.order(*order.uniq.reject{|o| o.blank?}) unless order.empty?
        
      280. 
      
        
    280. 
          
          
          
        
      281. 
      
        
    281. 
          13
          
                build_select(arel, @select_values.uniq)
        
      282. 
      
        
    282. 
          
          
          
        
      283. 
      
        
    283. 
          13
          
                arel.distinct(@uniq_value)
        
      284. 
      
        
    284. 
          13
          
                arel.from(@from_value) if @from_value
        
      285. 
      
        
    285. 
          13
          
                arel.lock(@lock_value) if @lock_value
        
      286.

      287.

                arel

          1
          
              def custom_join_ast(table, joins)
        
      293. 
      
        
    293. 
          
          
                joins = joins.reject { |join| join.blank? }
        
      294. 
      
        
    294. 
          
          
          
        
      295. 
      
        
    295. 
          
          
                return [] if joins.empty?
        
      296. 
      
        
    296. 
          
          
          
        
      297. 
      
        
    297. 
          
          
                @implicit_readonly = true
        
      298. 
      
        
    298. 
          
          
          
        
      299. 
      
        
    299. 
          
          
                joins.map do |join|
        
      300. 
      
        
    300. 
          
          
                  case join
        
      301. 
      
        
    301. 
          
          
                  when Array
        
      302. 
      
        
    302. 
          
          
                    join = Arel.sql(join.join(' ')) if array_of_strings?(join)
        
      303. 
      
        
    303. 
          
          
                  when String
        
      304. 
      
        
    304. 
          
          
                    join = Arel.sql(join)
        
      305. 
      
        
    305. 
          
          
                  end
        
      306. 
      
        
    306. 
          
          
                  table.create_string_join(join)
        
      307. 
      
        
    307. 
          
          
                end
        
      308. 
      
        
    308. 
          
          
              end
        
      309. 
      
        
    309. 
          
          
          
        
      310. 
      
        
    310. 
          1
          
              def collapse_wheres(arel, wheres)
        
      311. 
      
        
    311. 
          13
          
                equalities = wheres.grep(Arel::Nodes::Equality)
        
      312. 
      
        
    312. 
          
          
          
        
      313. 
      
        
    313. 
          13
          
                arel.where(Arel::Nodes::And.new(equalities)) unless equalities.empty?
        
      314. 
      
        
    314. 
          
          
          
        
      315. 
      
        
    315. 
          13
          
                (wheres - equalities).each do |where|
        
      316. 
      
        
    316. 
          
          
                  where = Arel.sql(where) if String === where
        
      317. 
      
        
    317. 
          
          
                  arel.where(Arel::Nodes::Grouping.new(where))
        
      318. 
      
        
    318. 
          
          
                end
        
      319. 
      
        
    319. 
          
          
              end
        
      320. 
      
        
    320. 
          
          
          
        
      321. 
      
        
    321. 
          1
          
              def build_where(opts, other = [])
        
      322. 
      
        
    322. 
          10
          
                case opts
        
      323. 
      
        
    323. 
          
          
                when String, Array
        
      324. 
      
        
    324. 
          
          
                  [@klass.send(:sanitize_sql, other.empty? ? opts : ([opts] + other))]
        
      325. 
      
        
    325. 
          
          
                when Hash
        
      326. 
      
        
    326. 
          2
          
                  attributes = @klass.send(:expand_hash_conditions_for_aggregates, opts)
        
      327. 
      
        
    327. 
          2
          
                  PredicateBuilder.build_from_hash(table.engine, attributes, table)
        
      328. 
      
        
    328. 
          
          
                else
        
      329. 
      
        
    329. 
          8
          
                  [opts]
        
      330. 
      
        
    330. 
          
          
                end
        
      331. 
      
        
    331. 
          
          
              end
        
      332. 
      
        
    332. 
          
          
          
        
      333. 
      
        
    333. 
          1
          
              def build_joins(manager, joins)
        
      334. 
      
        
    334. 
          
          
                buckets = joins.group_by do |join|
        
      335. 
      
        
    335. 
          
          
                  case join
        
      336. 
      
        
    336. 
          
          
                  when String
        
      337. 
      
        
    337. 
          
          
                    'string_join'
        
      338. 
      
        
    338. 
          
          
                  when Hash, Symbol, Array
        
      339. 
      
        
    339. 
          
          
                    'association_join'
        
      340. 
      
        
    340. 
          
          
                  when ActiveRecord::Associations::JoinDependency::JoinAssociation
        
      341. 
      
        
    341. 
          
          
                    'stashed_join'
        
      342. 
      
        
    342. 
          
          
                  when Arel::Nodes::Join
        
      343. 
      
        
    343. 
          
          
                    'join_node'
        
      344. 
      
        
    344. 
          
          
                  else
        
      345. 
      
        
    345. 
          
          
                    raise 'unknown class: %s' % join.class.name
        
      346. 
      
        
    346. 
          
          
                  end
        
      347. 
      
        
    347. 
          
          
                end
        
      348. 
      
        
    348. 
          
          
          
        
      349. 
      
        
    349. 
          
          
                association_joins         = buckets['association_join'] || []
        
      350. 
      
        
    350. 
          
          
                stashed_association_joins = buckets['stashed_join'] || []
        
      351. 
      
        
    351. 
          
          
                join_nodes                = (buckets['join_node'] || []).uniq
        
      352. 
      
        
    352. 
          
          
                string_joins              = (buckets['string_join'] || []).map { |x|
        
      353. 
      
        
    353. 
          
          
                  x.strip
        
      354. 
      
        
    354. 
          
          
                }.uniq
        
      355. 
      
        
    355. 
          
          
          
        
      356. 
      
        
    356. 
          
          
                join_list = join_nodes + custom_join_ast(manager, string_joins)
        
      357. 
      
        
    357. 
          
          
          
        
      358. 
      
        
    358. 
          
          
                join_dependency = ActiveRecord::Associations::JoinDependency.new(
        
      359. 
      
        
    359. 
          
          
                  @klass,
        
      360. 
      
        
    360. 
          
          
                  association_joins,
        
      361. 
      
        
    361. 
          
          
                  join_list
        
      362. 
      
        
    362. 
          
          
                )
        
      363. 
      
        
    363. 
          
          
          
        
      364. 
      
        
    364. 
          
          
                join_dependency.graft(*stashed_association_joins)
        
      365. 
      
        
    365. 
          
          
          
        
      366. 
      
        
    366. 
          
          
                @implicit_readonly = true unless association_joins.empty? && stashed_association_joins.empty?
        
      367. 
      
        
    367. 
          
          
          
        
      368. 
      
        
    368. 
          
          
                # FIXME: refactor this to build an AST
        
      369. 
      
        
    369. 
          
          
                join_dependency.join_associations.each do |association|
        
      370. 
      
        
    370. 
          
          
                  association.join_to(manager)
        
      371. 
      
        
    371. 
          
          
                end
        
      372. 
      
        
    372. 
          
          
          
        
      373. 
      
        
    373. 
          
          
                manager.join_sources.concat join_list
        
      374. 
      
        
    374. 
          
          
          
        
      375. 
      
        
    375. 
          
          
                manager
        
      376. 
      
        
    376. 
          
          
              end
        
      377. 
      
        
    377. 
          
          
          
        
      378. 
      
        
    378. 
          1
          
              def build_select(arel, selects)
        
      379. 
      
        
    379. 
          13
          
                unless selects.empty?
        
      380. 
      
        
    380. 
          6
          
                  @implicit_readonly = false
        
      381. 
      
        
    381. 
          6
          
                  arel.project(*selects)
        
      382. 
      
        
    382. 
          
          
                else
        
      383. 
      
        
    383. 
          7
          
                  arel.project(@klass.arel_table[Arel.star])
        
      384. 
      
        
    384. 
          
          
                end
        
      385. 
      
        
    385. 
          
          
              end
        
      386. 
      
        
    386. 
          
          
          
        
      387. 
      
        
    387. 
          1
          
              def apply_modules(modules)
        
      388. 
      
        
    388. 
          12
          
                unless modules.empty?
        
      389. 
      
        
    389. 
          
          
                  @extensions += modules
        
      390. 
      
        
    390. 
          
          
                  modules.each {|extension| extend(extension) }
        
      391. 
      
        
    391. 
          
          
                end
        
      392. 
      
        
    392. 
          
          
              end
        
      393. 
      
        
    393. 
          
          
          
        
      394. 
      
        
    394. 
          1
          
              def reverse_sql_order(order_query)
        
      395. 
      
        
    395. 
          
          
                order_query = ["#{quoted_table_name}.#{quoted_primary_key} ASC"] if order_query.empty?
        
      396. 
      
        
    396. 
          
          
          
        
      397. 
      
        
    397. 
          
          
                order_query.map do |o|
        
      398. 
      
        
    398. 
          
          
                  case o
        
      399. 
      
        
    399. 
          
          
                  when Arel::Nodes::Ordering
        
      400. 
      
        
    400. 
          
          
                    o.reverse
        
      401. 
      
        
    401. 
          
          
                  when String, Symbol

                # Works just like <tt>String#split</tt>, with the exception that the items in the resulting list are Chars

          1
          
                def split(*args)

      252.

      253. 
      
        
    253. 
          
          
                # Like <tt>String#[]=</tt>, except instead of byte offsets you specify character offsets.
        
      254. 
      
        
    254. 
          
          
                #
        
      255. 
      
        
    255. 
          
          
                # Example:
        
      256.

      257.

      259. 
      
        
    259.

      260.

      261.

                #   s = "Mller"
        
      263. 
      
        
    263. 
          
          
                #   s.mb_chars[1, 2] = "" # Replace 2 characters at character offset 1
        
      264. 
      
        
    264. 
          
          
                #   s
        
      265. 
      
        
    265. 
          
          
                #   # => "Mler"
        
      266. 
      
        
    266. 
          1
          
                def []=(*args)
        
      267. 
      
        
    267. 
          
          
                  replace_by = args.pop
        
      268. 
      
        
    268. 
          
          
                  # Indexed replace with regular expressions already works
        
      269. 
      
        
    269. 
          
          
                  if args.first.is_a?(Regexp)
        
      270. 
      
        
    270. 
          
          
                    @wrapped_string[*args] = replace_by
        
      271. 
      
        
    271. 
          
          
                  else
        
      272. 
      
        
    272. 
          
          
                    result = Unicode.u_unpack(@wrapped_string)
        
      273. 
      
        
    273. 
          
          
                    case args.first
        
      274. 
      
        
    274. 
          
          
                    when Fixnum
        
      275. 
      
        
    275. 
          
          
                      raise IndexError, "index #{args[0]} out of string" if args[0] >= result.length
        
      276. 
      
        
    276. 
          
          
                      min = args[0]
        
      277. 
      
        
    277. 
          
          
                      max = args[1].nil? ? min : (min + args[1] - 1)
        
      278. 
      
        
    278. 
          
          
                      range = Range.new(min, max)
        
      279. 
      
        
    279. 
          
          
                      replace_by = [replace_by].pack('U') if replace_by.is_a?(Fixnum)
        
      280. 
      
        
    280. 
          
          
                    when Range
        
      281. 
      
        
    281. 
          
          
                      raise RangeError, "#{args[0]} out of range" if args[0].min >= result.length
        
      282. 
      
        
    282. 
          
          
                      range = args[0]
        
      283. 
      
        
    283. 
          
          
                    else
        
      284. 
      
        
    284. 
          
          
                      needle = args[0].to_s
        
      285. 
      
        
    285. 
          
          
                      min = index(needle)
        
      286. 
      
        
    286. 
          
          
                      max = min + Unicode.u_unpack(needle).length - 1
        
      287. 
      
        
    287. 
          
          
                      range = Range.new(min, max)
        
      288. 
      
        
    288. 
          
          
                    end
        
      289. 
      
        
    289. 
          
          
                    result[range] = Unicode.u_unpack(replace_by)
        
      290. 
      
        
    290. 
          
          
                    @wrapped_string.replace(result.pack('U*'))
        
      291. 
      
        
    291. 
          
          
                  end
        
      292. 
      
        
    292. 
          
          
                end
        
      293. 
      
        
    293. 
          
          
          
        
      294. 
      
        
    294. 
          
          
                # Reverses all characters in the string.
        
      295. 
      
        
    295. 
          
          
                #
        
      296. 
      
        
    296. 
          
          
                # Example:
        
      297. 
      
        
    297. 
          
          
                #   'Caf'.mb_chars.reverse.to_s # => 'faC'
        
      298. 
      
        
    298. 
          1
          
                def reverse
        
      299. 
      
        
    299. 
          
          
                  chars(Unicode.g_unpack(@wrapped_string).reverse.flatten.pack('U*'))
        
      300. 
      
        
    300. 
          
          
                end
        
      301.

      302. 
      
        
    302. 
          
          
                # Implements Unicode-aware slice with codepoints. Slicing on one point returns the codepoints for that
        
      303. 
      
        
    303. 
          
          
                # character.
        
      304. 
      
        
    304. 
          
          
                #
        
      305. 
      
        
    305. 
          
          
                # Example:
        
      306. 
      
        
    306. 
          
          
                #   ''.mb_chars.slice(2..3).to_s # => ""
        
      307. 
      
        
    307. 
          1
          
                def slice(*args)
        
      308. 
      
        
    308. 
          6
          
                  if args.size > 2
        
      309. 
      
        
    309. 
          
          
                    raise ArgumentError, "wrong number of arguments (#{args.size} for 1)" # Do as if we were native
        
      310.

                  def justify(integer, way, padstr=' ') #:nodoc:
        
      447. 
      
        
    447. 
          
          
                    raise ArgumentError, "zero width padding" if padstr.length == 0

      459.

      460. 
      
        
    460.

      461.

                    raise EncodingError, 'malformed UTF-8 character'
        
      74. 
      
        
    74. 
          
          
                  end
        
      75. 
      
        
    75. 
          
          
                end
        
      76. 
      
        
    76. 
          
          
          
        
      77. 
      
        
    77. 
          
          
                # Detect whether the codepoint is in a certain character class. Returns +true+ when it's in the specified
        
      78. 
      
        
    78. 
          
          
                # character class and +false+ otherwise. Valid character classes are: <tt>:cr</tt>, <tt>:lf</tt>, <tt>:l</tt>,
        
      79. 
      
        
    79. 
          
          
                # <tt>:v</tt>, <tt>:lv</tt>, <tt>:lvt</tt> and <tt>:t</tt>.
        
      80. 
      
        
    80. 
          
          
                #
        
      81. 
      
        
    81. 
          
          
                # Primarily used by the grapheme cluster support.
        
      82. 
      
        
    82. 
          1
          
                def in_char_class?(codepoint, classes)
        
      83. 
      
        
    83. 
          
          
                  classes.detect { |c| database.boundary[c] === codepoint } ? true : false
        
      84. 
      
        
    84. 
          
          
                end
        
      85. 
      
        
    85. 
          
          
          
        
      86. 
      
        
    86. 
          
          
                # Unpack the string at grapheme boundaries. Returns a list of character lists.
        
      87. 
      
        
    87. 
          
          
                #
        
      88. 
      
        
    88. 
          
          
                # Example:
        
      89. 
      
        
    89. 
          
          
                #   Unicode.g_unpack('') # => [[2325, 2381], [2359], [2367]]
        
      90. 
      
        
    90. 
          
          
                #   Unicode.g_unpack('Caf') # => [[67], [97], [102], [233]]
        
      91. 
      
        
    91. 
          1
          
                def g_unpack(string)
        
      92. 
      
        
    92. 
          
          
                  codepoints = u_unpack(string)
        
      93. 
      
        
    93. 
          
          
                  unpacked = []
        
      94. 
      
        
    94. 
          
          
                  pos = 0
        
      95. 
      
        
    95. 
          
          
                  marker = 0
        
      96. 
      
        
    96. 
          
          
                  eoc = codepoints.length
        
      97. 
      
        
    97. 
          
          
                  while(pos < eoc)
        
      98. 
      
        
    98. 
          
          
                    pos += 1
        
      99. 
      
        
    99. 
          
          
                    previous = codepoints[pos-1]
        
      100. 
      
        
    100. 
          
          
                    current = codepoints[pos]
        
      101. 
      
        
    101. 
          
          
                    if (
        
      102. 
      
        
    102. 
          
          
                        # CR X LF
        
      103. 
      
        
    103. 
          
          
                        ( previous == database.boundary[:cr] and current == database.boundary[:lf] ) or
        
      104. 
      
        
    104. 
          
          
                        # L X (L|V|LV|LVT)
        
      105. 
      
        
    105. 
          
          
                        ( database.boundary[:l] === previous and in_char_class?(current, [:l,:v,:lv,:lvt]) ) or
        
      106. 
      
        
    106. 
          
          
                        # (LV|V) X (V|T)
        
      107. 
      
        
    107. 
          
          
                        ( in_char_class?(previous, [:lv,:v]) and in_char_class?(current, [:v,:t]) ) or
        
      108. 
      
        
    108. 
          
          
                        # (LVT|T) X (T)
        
      109. 
      
        
    109. 
          
          
                        ( in_char_class?(previous, [:lvt,:t]) and database.boundary[:t] === current ) or
        
      110. 
      
        
    110. 
          
          
                        # X Extend
        
      111. 
      
        
    111. 
          
          
                        (database.boundary[:extend] === current)
        
      112. 
      
        
    112. 
          
          
                      )
        
      113. 
      
        
    113. 
          
          
                    else
        
      114. 
      
        
    114. 
          
          
                      unpacked << codepoints[marker..pos-1]
        
      115. 
      
        
    115. 
          
          
                      marker = pos
        
      116. 
      
        
    116. 
          
          
                    end
        
      117. 
      
        
    117. 
          
          
                  end
        
      118. 
      
        
    118. 
          
          
                  unpacked
        
      119. 
      
        
    119. 
          
          
                end
        
      120. 
      
        
    120. 
          
          
          
        
      121. 
      
        
    121. 
          
          
                # Reverse operation of g_unpack.
        
      122. 
      
        
    122. 
          
          
                #
        
      123. 
      
        
    123. 
          
          
                # Example:
        
      124. 
      
        
    124. 
          
          
                #   Unicode.g_pack(Unicode.g_unpack('')) # => ''
        
      125. 
      
        
    125. 
          1
          
                def g_pack(unpacked)
        
      126. 
      
        
    126. 
          
          
                  (unpacked.flatten).pack('U*')
        
      127. 
      
        
    127. 
          
          
                end
        
      128. 
      
        
    128. 
          
          
          
        
      129. 
      
        
    129. 
          
          
                # Re-order codepoints so the string becomes canonical.
        
      130. 
      
        
    130. 
          1
          
                def reorder_characters(codepoints)
        
      131. 
      
        
    131. 
          
          
                  length = codepoints.length- 1
        
      132. 
      
        
    132. 
          
          
                  pos = 0
        
      133. 
      
        
    133. 
          
          
                  while pos < length do
        
      134. 
      
        
    134. 
          
          
                    cp1, cp2 = database.codepoints[codepoints[pos]], database.codepoints[codepoints[pos+1]]
        
      135. 
      
        
    135. 
          
          
                    if (cp1.combining_class > cp2.combining_class) && (cp2.combining_class > 0)
        
      136. 
      
        
    136. 
          
          
                      codepoints[pos..pos+1] = cp2.code, cp1.code
        
      137. 
      
        
    137. 
          
          
                      pos += (pos > 0 ? -1 : 1)
        
      138. 
      
        
    138. 
          
          
                    else
        
      139. 
      
        
    139. 
          
          
                      pos += 1
        
      140. 
      
        
    140. 
          
          
                    end
        
      141. 
      
        
    141. 
          
          
                  end
        
      142. 
      
        
    142. 
          
          
                  codepoints
        
      143. 
      
        
    143. 
          
          
                end
        
      144. 
      
        
    144. 
          
          
          
        
      145. 
      
        
    145. 
          
          
                # Decompose composed characters to the decomposed form.
        
      146. 
      
        
    146. 
          1
          
                def decompose_codepoints(type, codepoints)
        
      147. 
      
        
    147. 
          
          
                  codepoints.inject([]) do |decomposed, cp|
        
      148. 
      
        
    148. 
          
          
                    # if it's a hangul syllable starter character
        
      149. 
      
        
    149. 
          
          
                    if HANGUL_SBASE <= cp and cp < HANGUL_SLAST
        
      150. 
      
        
    150. 
          
          
                      sindex = cp - HANGUL_SBASE
        
      151. 
      
        
    151. 
          
          
                      ncp = [] # new codepoints
        
      152. 
      
        
    152. 
          
          
                      ncp << HANGUL_LBASE + sindex / HANGUL_NCOUNT
        
      153. 
      
        
    153. 
          
          
                      ncp << HANGUL_VBASE + (sindex % HANGUL_NCOUNT) / HANGUL_TCOUNT
        
      154. 
      
        
    154. 
          
          
                      tindex = sindex % HANGUL_TCOUNT
        
      155. 
      
        
    155. 
          
          
                      ncp << (HANGUL_TBASE + tindex) unless tindex == 0
        
      156. 
      
        
    156. 
          
          
                      decomposed.concat ncp
        
      157. 
      
        
    157. 
          
          
                    # if the codepoint is decomposable in with the current decomposition type
        
      158. 
      
        
    158. 
          
          
                    elsif (ncp = database.codepoints[cp].decomp_mapping) and (!database.codepoints[cp].decomp_type || type == :compatability)
        
      159. 
      
        
    159. 
          
          
                      decomposed.concat decompose_codepoints(type, ncp.dup)
        
      160. 
      
        
    160. 
          
          
                    else
        
      161. 
      
        
    161. 
          
          
                      decomposed << cp
        
      162. 
      
        
    162. 
          
          
                    end
        
      163. 
      
        
    163. 
          
          
                  end
        
      164. 
      
        
    164. 
          
          
                end
        
      165. 
      
        
    165. 
          
          
          
        
      166. 
      
        
    166. 
          
          
                # Compose decomposed characters to the composed form.
        
      167. 
      
        
    167. 
          1
          
                def compose_codepoints(codepoints)
        
      168. 
      
        
    168. 
          
          
                  pos = 0
        
      169. 
      
        
    169. 
          
          
                  eoa = codepoints.length - 1
        
      170. 
      
        
    170. 
          
          
                  starter_pos = 0
        
      171. 
      
        
    171. 
          
          
                  starter_char = codepoints[0]
        
      172. 
      
        
    172. 
          
          
                  previous_combining_class = -1
        
      173. 
      
        
    173. 
          
          
                  while pos < eoa
        
      174. 
      
        
    174. 
          
          
                    pos += 1
        
      175. 
      
        
    175. 
          
          
                    lindex = starter_char - HANGUL_LBASE
        
      176. 
      
        
    176. 
          
          
                    # -- Hangul
        
      177. 
      
        
    177. 
          
          
                    if 0 <= lindex and lindex < HANGUL_LCOUNT
        
      178. 
      
        
    178. 
          
          
                      vindex = codepoints[starter_pos+1] - HANGUL_VBASE rescue vindex = -1
        
      179. 
      
        
    179. 
          
          
                      if 0 <= vindex and vindex < HANGUL_VCOUNT
        
      180. 
      
        
    180. 
          
          
                        tindex = codepoints[starter_pos+2] - HANGUL_TBASE rescue tindex = -1
        
      181. 
      
        
    181. 
          
          
                        if 0 <= tindex and tindex < HANGUL_TCOUNT
        
      182. 
      
        
    182. 
          
          
                          j = starter_pos + 2
        
      183. 
      
        
    183. 
          
          
                          eoa -= 2
        
      184. 
      
        
    184. 
          
          
                        else
        
      185. 
      
        
    185. 
          
          
                          tindex = 0
        
      186. 
      
        
    186. 
          
          
                          j = starter_pos + 1
        
      187. 
      
        
    187. 
          
          
                          eoa -= 1
        
      188. 
      
        
    188. 
          
          
                        end
        
      189. 
      
        
    189. 
          
          
                        codepoints[starter_pos..j] = (lindex * HANGUL_VCOUNT + vindex) * HANGUL_TCOUNT + tindex + HANGUL_SBASE
        
      190. 
      
        
    190. 
          
          
                      end
        
      191. 
      
        
    191. 
          
          
                      starter_pos += 1
        
      192. 
      
        
    192. 
          
          
                      starter_char = codepoints[starter_pos]
        
      193. 
      
        
    193. 
          
          
                    # -- Other characters
        
      194. 
      
        
    194. 
          
          
                    else
        
      195. 
      
        
    195. 
          
          
                      current_char = codepoints[pos]
        
      196. 
      
        
    196. 
          
          
                      current = database.codepoints[current_char]
        
      197. 
      
        
    197. 
          
          
                      if current.combining_class > previous_combining_class
        
      198. 
      
        
    198. 
          
          
                        if ref = database.composition_map[starter_char]
        
      199. 
      
        
    199. 
          
          
                          composition = ref[current_char]
        
      200. 
      
        
    200. 
          
          
                        else
        
      201. 
      
        
    201. 
          
          
                          composition = nil
        
      202. 
      
        
    202. 
          
          
                        end
        
      203. 
      
        
    203. 
          
          
                        unless composition.nil?
        
      204. 
      
        
    204. 
          
          
                          codepoints[starter_pos] = composition
        
      205. 
      
        
    205. 
          
          
                          starter_char = composition
        
      206. 
      
        
    206. 
          
          
                          codepoints.delete_at pos
        
      207. 
      
        
    207. 
          
          
                          eoa -= 1
        
      208. 
      
        
    208. 
          
          
                          pos -= 1
        
      209. 
      
        
    209. 
          
          
                          previous_combining_class = -1
        
      210. 
      
        
    210. 
          
          
                        else
        
      211. 
      
        
    211. 
          
          
                          previous_combining_class = current.combining_class
        
      212. 
      
        
    212. 
          
          
                        end
        
      213. 
      
        
    213. 
          
          
                      else
        
      214. 
      
        
    214. 
          
          
                        previous_combining_class = current.combining_class
        
      215. 
      
        
    215. 
          
          
                      end
        
      216. 
      
        
    216. 
          
          
                      if current.combining_class == 0
        
      217. 
      
        
    217. 
          
          
                        starter_pos = pos
        
      218. 
      
        
    218. 
          
          
                        starter_char = codepoints[pos]
        
      219. 
      
        
    219. 
          
          
                      end
        
      220. 
      
        
    220. 
          
          
                    end
        
      221. 
      
        
    221. 
          
          
                  end
        
      222. 
      
        
    222. 
          
          
                  codepoints
        
      223. 
      
        
    223. 
          
          
                end
        
      224. 
      
        
    224. 
          
          
          
        
      225. 
      
        
    225. 
          
          
                # Replaces all ISO-8859-1 or CP1252 characters by their UTF-8 equivalent resulting in a valid UTF-8 string.
        
      226. 
      
        
    226. 
          
          
                #
        
      227. 
      
        
    227. 
          
          
                # Passing +true+ will forcibly tidy all bytes, assuming that the string's encoding is entirely CP1252 or ISO-8859-1.
        
      228. 
      
        
    228. 
          1
          
                def tidy_bytes(string, force = false)
        
      229. 
      
        
    229. 
          
          
                  if force
        
      230. 
      
        
    230. 
          
          
                    return string.unpack("C*").map do |b|
        
      231. 
      
        
    231. 
          
          
                      tidy_byte(b)
        
      232. 
      
        
    232. 
          
          
                    end.flatten.compact.pack("C*").unpack("U*").pack("U*")
        
      233. 
      
        
    233. 
          
          
                  end
        
      234. 
      
        
    234. 
          
          
          
        
      235. 
      
        
    235. 
          
          
                  bytes = string.unpack("C*")
        
      236. 
      
        
    236. 
          
          
                  conts_expected = 0
        
      237. 
      
        
    237. 
          
          
                  last_lead = 0
        
      238. 
      
        
    238. 
          
          
          
        
      239. 
      
        
    239. 
          
          
                  bytes.each_index do |i|
        
      240. 
      
        
    240. 
          
          
          
        
      241. 
      
        
    241. 
          
          
                    byte          = bytes[i]
        
      242. 
      
        
    242. 
          
          
                    is_cont       = byte > 127 && byte < 192
        
      243. 
      
        
    243. 
          
          
                    is_lead       = byte > 191 && byte < 245
        
      244. 
      
        
    244. 
          
          
                    is_unused     = byte > 240
        
      245. 
      
        
    245. 
          
          
                    is_restricted = byte > 244
        
      246. 
      
        
    246. 
          
          
          
        
      247. 
      
        
    247. 
          
          
                    # Impossible or highly unlikely byte? Clean it.
        
      248. 
      
        
    248. 
          
          
                    if is_unused || is_restricted
        
      249. 
      
        
    249. 
          
          
                      bytes[i] = tidy_byte(byte)
        
      250. 
      
        
    250. 
          
          
                    elsif is_cont
        
      251. 
      
        
    251. 
          
          
                      # Not expecting continuation byte? Clean up. Otherwise, now expect one less.
        
      252. 
      
        
    252. 
          
          
                      conts_expected == 0 ? bytes[i] = tidy_byte(byte) : conts_expected -= 1
        
      253. 
      
        
    253. 
          
          
                    else
        
      254. 
      
        
    254. 
          
          
                      if conts_expected > 0
        
      255. 
      
        
    255. 
          
          
                        # Expected continuation, but got ASCII or leading? Clean backwards up to
        
      256. 
      
        
    256. 
          
          
                        # the leading byte.
        
      257. 
      
        
    257. 
          
          
                        (1..(i - last_lead)).each {|j| bytes[i - j] = tidy_byte(bytes[i - j])}
        
      258. 
      
        
    258. 
          
          
                        conts_expected = 0
        
      259. 
      
        
    259. 
          
          
                      end
        
      260. 
      
        
    260. 
          
          
                      if is_lead
        
      261. 
      
        
    261. 
          
          
                        # Final byte is leading? Clean it.
        
      262. 
      
        
    262. 
          
          
                        if i == bytes.length - 1
        
      263. 
      
        
    263. 
          
          
                          bytes[i] = tidy_byte(bytes.last)
        
      264. 
      
        
    264. 
          
          
                        else
        
      265. 
      
        
    265. 
          
          
                          # Valid leading byte? Expect continuations determined by position of
        
      266. 
      
        
    266. 
          
          
                          # first zero bit, with max of 3.
        
      267. 
      
        
    267. 
          
          
                          conts_expected = byte < 224 ? 1 : byte < 240 ? 2 : 3
        
      268. 
      
        
    268. 
          
          
                          last_lead = i
        
      269. 
      
        
    269. 
          
          
                        end
        
      270. 
      
        
    270. 
          
          
                      end
        
      271. 
      
        
    271. 
          
          
                    end
        
      272. 
      
        
    272. 
          
          
                  end
        
      273. 
      
        
    273. 
          
          
                  bytes.empty? ? "" : bytes.flatten.compact.pack("C*").unpack("U*").pack("U*")
        
      274. 
      
        
    274. 
          
          
                end
        
      275. 
      
        
    275. 
          
          
          
        
      276. 
      
        
    276. 
          
          
                # Returns the KC normalization of the string by default. NFKC is considered the best normalization form for
        
      277. 
      
        
    277. 
          
          
                # passing strings to databases and validations.
        
      278. 
      
        
    278. 
          
          
                #
        
      279. 
      
        
    279. 
          
          
                # * <tt>string</tt> - The string to perform normalization on.
        
      280. 
      
        
    280. 
          
          
                # * <tt>form</tt> - The form you want to normalize in. Should be one of the following:
        
      281. 
      
        
    281. 
          
          
                #   <tt>:c</tt>, <tt>:kc</tt>, <tt>:d</tt>, or <tt>:kd</tt>. Default is
        
      282. 
      
        
    282. 
          
          
                #   ActiveSupport::Multibyte.default_normalization_form
        
      283. 
      
        
    283. 
          1
          
                def normalize(string, form=nil)
        
      284. 
      
        
    284. 
          
          
                  form ||= @default_normalization_form
        
      285. 
      
        
    285. 
          
          
                  # See http://www.unicode.org/reports/tr15, Table 1
        
      286. 
      
        
    286. 
          
          
                  codepoints = u_unpack(string)
        
      287. 
      
        
    287. 
          
          
                  case form
        
      288. 
      
        
    288. 
          
          
                    when :d
        
      289. 
      
        
    289. 
          
          
                      reorder_characters(decompose_codepoints(:canonical, codepoints))
        
      290. 
      
        
    290. 
          
          
                    when :c
        
      291. 
      
        
    291. 
          
          
                      compose_codepoints(reorder_characters(decompose_codepoints(:canonical, codepoints)))
        
      292. 
      
        
    292. 
          
          
                    when :kd
        
      293. 
      
        
    293. 
          
          
                      reorder_characters(decompose_codepoints(:compatability, codepoints))
        
      294. 
      
        
    294. 
          
          
                    when :kc
        
      295. 
      
        
    295. 
          
          
                      compose_codepoints(reorder_characters(decompose_codepoints(:compatability, codepoints)))
        
      296. 
      
        
    296. 
          
          
                    else
        
      297. 
      
        
    297. 
          
          
                      raise ArgumentError, "#{form} is not a valid normalization variant", caller
        
      298. 
      
        
    298. 
          
          
                  end.pack('U*')
        
      299. 
      
        
    299. 
          
          
                end
        
      300. 
      
        
    300. 
          
          
          
        
      301. 
      
        
    301. 
          1
          
                def apply_mapping(string, mapping) #:nodoc:
        
      302. 
      
        
    302. 
          
          
                  u_unpack(string).map do |codepoint|
        
      303. 
      
        
    303. 
          
          
                    cp = database.codepoints[codepoint]
        
      304. 
      
        
    304. 
          
          
                    if cp and (ncp = cp.send(mapping)) and ncp > 0
        
      305. 
      
        
    305. 
          
          
                      ncp
        
      306. 
      
        
    306. 
          
          
                    else
        
      307. 
      
        
    307. 
          
          
                      codepoint
        
      308. 
      
        
    308. 
          
          
                    end
        
      309. 
      
        
    309. 
          
          
                  end.pack('U*')
        
      310. 
      
        
    310. 
          
          
                end
        
      311. 
      
        
    311. 
          
          
          
        
      312. 
      
        
    312. 
          
          
                # Holds data about a codepoint in the Unicode database
        
      313. 
      
        
    313. 
          1
          
                class Codepoint
        
      314. 
      
        
    314. 
          1
          
                  attr_accessor :code, :combining_class, :decomp_type, :decomp_mapping, :uppercase_mapping, :lowercase_mapping
        
      315. 
      
        
    315. 
          
          
                end
        
      316. 
      
        
    316. 
          
          
          
        
      317. 
      
        
    317. 
          
          
                # Holds static data from the Unicode database
        
      318. 
      
        
    318. 
          1
          
                class UnicodeDatabase
        
      319. 
      
        
    319. 
          1
          
                  ATTRIBUTES = :codepoints, :composition_exclusion, :composition_map, :boundary, :cp1252
        
      320. 
      
        
    320. 
          
          
          
        
      321. 
      
        
    321. 
          1
          
                  attr_writer(*ATTRIBUTES)
        
      322. 
      
        
    322. 
          
          
          
        
      323. 
      
        
    323. 
          1
          
                  def initialize
